This race condition was present in hub.go.
Two Race conditions were there - 

1)Unprotected global variable - count

2)Race on message variable 

Conditions were eliminated by using lock synchronization.

Here is the code - 

for subscriber := range h.registry {
		sub := subscriber
		if sub.Match(message.Topic()) {
			wg.Add(1)
			go func(mRoutine Message) {
				countMu.Lock() //Locking before Increment of count
                                count += sub.Publish(mRoutine)
				countMu.Unlock()
                                wg.Done()
			}(message)
		}
	}


Planning to use Atomic Increments also to see if they are more efficient

==================


Race condition was present in event.go.

Unlock statement was not being deferred in function causing race condition.


Buggy code - 

        s.Lock()
	
	_, exists := s.clients[id]
	if !exists {
		s.clients[id] = s.Subscribe("system:")
	}

        s.Unlock()
       return s.clients[id], exists




Solution - 

       s.Lock()
       defer s.Unlock()
	_, exists := s.clients[id]
	if !exists {
		s.clients[id] = s.Subscribe("system:")
	}

       return s.clients[id], exists
    

General solution illustration in this case -

        package main

import (
   "sync"
 
)

var mutexv1 sync.RWMutex


var service map[int]int = make(map[int]int)


func procesmap(i int) int{
		mutexv1.Lock()
		
                service[i] = 1

               	mutexv1.Unlock() 	

		return service[i]
	}

func main() {
         
       
        
	go procesmap(1)
	
	go procesmap(2)


}


         deferring unlock statement is the solution

Race condition in Subscriber.go

Solution Code -

Read lock has been added for go routines.

func (s *ethSubscriber) Match(topic string) bool {
	s.mutex.RLock()
	defer s.mutex.RUnlock()
        events := types.EventData{}
	if err := proto.Unmarshal([]byte(topic), &events); err != nil {
		return false
	}

	return utils.MatchEthFilter(s.filter, events)
}

Lock synchronization has been added

func (s *ethSubscriber) Do(sf pubsub.SubscriberFunc) pubsub.Subscriber {
	s.mutex.Lock()
	defer s.mutex.Unlock()
        s.sf = sf
	return s
}

Race condition in subscriber.go


Lock synchronization has been added 


func (s *ethSubscriber) Subscribe(topics ...string) pubsub.Subscriber {
	s.mutex.Lock()
	defer s.mutex.Unlock()
        var topic []byte
	if len(topics) > 0 {
		topic = []byte(topics[0])
	} else {
		topic = []byte{}
	}
	filter, err := utils.UnmarshalEthFilter(topic)
	if err == nil {
		s.filter = filter.EthBlockFilter
	}

	return s
}

Race condition in subscriber.go

Solution code - 

Read Lock synchronization has been added

func (s *ethSubscriber) Publish(message pubsub.Message) int {
	s.mutex.RLock()
	defer s.mutex.RUnlock()
   
        if s.sf == nil {
		return 0
	}
	ethMsg := types.EthMessage{
		Body: message.Body(),
		Id:   s.id,
	}
	msg, err := proto.Marshal(&ethMsg)
	if err != nil {
		return 0
	}
	s.sf(pubsub.NewMessage(message.Topic(), msg))
	return 1
}

Solution code - 

Read Lock synchronization has been added

func (s *ethSubscriber) Publish(message pubsub.Message) int {
	s.mutex.RLock()
	defer s.mutex.RUnlock()
   
        if s.sf == nil {
		return 0
	}
	ethMsg := types.EthMessage{
		Body: message.Body(),
		Id:   s.id,
	}
	msg, err := proto.Marshal(&ethMsg)
	if err != nil {
		return 0
	}
	s.sf(pubsub.NewMessage(message.Topic(), msg))
	return 1
}

Race condition in app.go 


// Commit commits the current block
func (a *Application) Commit() abci.ResponseCommit {
	var err error
        a.mutex.Lock()
	defer a.mutex.Unlock()

	defer func(begin time.Time) {
		lvs := []string{"method", "Commit", "error", fmt.Sprint(err != nil)}
		committedBlockCount.With(lvs...).Add(1)
		commitBlockLatency.With(lvs...).Observe(time.Since(begin).Seconds())
	}(time.Now())
	appHash, _, err := a.Store.SaveVersion()
	if err != nil {
		panic(err)
	}

	height := a.curBlockHeader.GetHeight()
	a.EventHandler.EmitBlockTx(uint64(height))
	a.EventHandler.EthSubscriptionSet().EmitBlockEvent(a.curBlockHeader)
	a.lastBlockHeader = a.curBlockHeader

	if err := a.Store.Prune(); err != nil {
		log.Error("failed to prune app.db", "err", err)
	}

	return abci.ResponseCommit{
		Data: appHash,
	}
}




func (a *Application) ReadOnlyState() State {
	a.mutex.Lock()
	defer a.mutex.Unlock()
        return NewStoreState(
		nil,
		a.Store,
		a.lastBlockHeader,
		nil,
	)
}
